28/09/24, 3:15 pm - Srushtiii: Intent Setup
Define these intents in Oracle Digital Assistant for handling the different categories:

GreetingIntent: Handles the initial greeting and introduction.

Sample Utterances:
"Hi"
"Hello"
"Hey"
CategoryIntent: Recognizes when the user needs to select an issue category.

Sample Utterances:
"I have an issue"
"I need help with something"
"I want assistance"
OrderIssueIntent: Handles issues related to orders.

Sample Utterances:
"I have a problem with my order"
"My order is delayed"
PaymentIssueIntent: Deals with payment-related issues.

Sample Utterances:
"There is a payment issue"
"I was charged twice"
ProductInfoIntent: Helps users with product-related questions.

Sample Utterances:
"Tell me more about a product"
"I need product details"
OtherIssueIntent: Catches any other issues that don’t fit into predefined categories.

Sample Utterances:
"I have a different problem"
"It’s not listed here"

kela hi nhi. Mala matter la vadhvaicha navta and majhya sathi jitka abhi imp 
hota titkich manuu hi important hoti. Mala konalach loose navta karaicha mhoon
me chup rhlo, tumcha madhe kahi bollo nhi -- Aata mala sang ki maza kai chukla.

kahi zala aasel mhnoon ha aasa boltoy, hoil thik nantar.

karat hota sakal pasun...mhnoon chup baslo hoto.

17/03/25, 2:06 pm - Shaan🤴: ye document madhun he 10 questions most impotant ahe ya type madhe yenr : 

1. A car manufacturing firm is considering two suppliers for in-vehicle music systems. Given importance weights for factors such as sound quality, cost, delivery time, and brand cachet, calculate the weighted score for each supplier and justify which one should be selected.  

2. Compare and contrast the positioning strategies of three major soft drink brands (e.g. Coca-Cola, Pepsi, and Sprite). Discuss their points-of-difference (PODs), points-of-parity (POPs), and the role of perceptual maps and emotional branding in shaping consumer perceptions.  

3. A mobile phone manufacturer incurs fixed costs of Rs. 60,00,000 and variable costs of Rs. 30,00,000 for a production run of 1,000 units. If the company targets a 30% markup, determine the unit price using the cost-based pricing formula. Explain each step of your calculation.  

4. Design an effective Segmentation, Targeting, and Positioning (STP) strategy for launching a new luxury product (e.g. high-end watches by MNMLST). Identify key market segments, justify your target selection, and outline a positioning strategy using both rational and emotional branding components.  

5. Select a current product (for example, Wonderchef) and analyze its stage in the product life cycle. Describe strategies that could be adopted at this stage—such as product modification, market modification, or changes in marketing programs—to sustain or boost its market performance.  

6. Evaluate the benefits and drawbacks of intensive, selective, and exclusive distribution channel strategies. Using a brand example (e.g. Nykaa or Jaipur Watch Company), recommend the most suitable distribution strategy and justify your recommendation.  

7. As the product manager for a revolutionary washing machine that uses minimal water and advanced technology, propose a pricing strategy. Explain the process from selecting the pricing objective to determining demand, estimating costs, analyzing competitors, choosing a pricing method, and finalizing the price.  

8. Compare the consumer buying process with the B2B procurement process. Use examples (such as buying a desktop for personal use versus purchasing 100 desktops for a company) to highlight the key differences and discuss why these differences matter for marketers.  

9. For an online jewelry brand like Shyle, develop a comprehensive strategy to measure customer satisfaction and foster loyalty. Include methods for satisfaction measurement (e.g. surveys, mystery shopping) and outline loyalty initiatives (e.g. membership programs, frequency rewards).  

10. Develop an integrated promotion strategy for a premium organic skincare brand (e.g. The Tribe Concept). Describe the steps from identifying the target audience and setting communication objectives to designing the message, selecting channels, deciding on a media mix, and measuring campaign effectiveness.
